				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Livre d'orgue No.3 (Lebègue, Nicolas)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div><table style="padding:0.5em; margin-left:auto; margin-right:auto; background-color:rgb(245,245,245); width:70%; border:1px solid #a3bfb1"><tr><td width="42px" valign="top"><a href="/wiki/File:Ambox_notice.png" class="image"><img alt="Ambox notice.png" src="/images/c/c8/Ambox_notice.png" width="40" height="40" /></a></td><td align="center">
This page is <b>only</b> for <b>complete</b> editions and <b>multiple selections</b> from the collection here. For arrangements, new editions, and the like see (or create) separate pages for individual works linked in the <b>General Information</b> section below.</td></tr></table></div>
<div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>4 sections
<ol><li>10 Offertoires
</li><li>4 Simphonies
</li><li>9 Noëls, Les Cloches
</li><li>8 Élévations
</li></ol>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Publication
</th>
<td>1685
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Pieces&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Pieces</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_organ&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For organ</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_organ&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the organ</a></span>; <span class="expandline" title="8 more..."><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_1_player&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 1 player</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:For_2_trumpets%2C_2_trombones%2C_timpani_%28arr%29&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">For 2 trumpets, 2 trombones, timpani (arr)</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Scores_featuring_the_trumpet&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Scores featuring the trumpet</a></span>;
